			<div id="sticky" class="fl-col fl-node-61bb16c21819e fl-col-small fl-visible-desktop-medium sticky" data-node="61bb16c21819e">
	<div class="fl-col-content fl-node-content">		<div class="fl-module fl-module-rich-text fl-node-61bb1ebaa044b" data-node="61bb1ebaa044b">

	<p><strong>Jump to:</strong></p>

			<div class="fl-col fl-node-61bb16c2181a3 fl-col-has-cols" data-node="61bb16c2181a3">
	<div class="fl-col-content fl-node-content">		<div id="bcr" class="fl-module fl-module-heading fl-node-5f0ddc9a90b77" data-node="5f0ddc9a90b77">
	<div class="fl-module-content fl-node-content">
		<h2 class="fl-heading">
		<span class="fl-heading-text">Binding Corporate Rules and International Data Transfer Privacy Tools</span>
	</h2>
	</div>
</div>
<div class="fl-module fl-module-rich-text fl-node-5f0dd9016d828" data-node="5f0dd9016d828">
	<div class="fl-module-content fl-node-content">
		<div class="fl-rich-text">
	<p>Colt BCRs controller and processor have been approved by the European Data Protection Board (EDPB) August 02, 2021. The approval was published in the official Gazette of the EDPB on August 05, 2021 and ratified by the Spanish Data Protection Authority, as Colt ́s BCR leading Authority August 16, 2021. The EDPB approved the Privacy and GDPR compliance programme implemented by Colt across the whole group. The approved privacy programme is legally binding on every company of the group.</p>
<p>Colt's BCR Controller and Processor decisions are published at the <a href="https://edpb.europa.eu/our-work-tools/accountability-tools/bcr_en">European Data Protection Board (EDPB) website</a>&nbsp;and in the<a href="https://www.aepd.es/es/documento/ti-00003-2021-resolucion-aprobacion-bcr-responsable-colt.pdf"> Spanish Data Protection Authority (“AEPD”) website.</a></p>
<p>You will be able to find the BCR approval document available on the <a href="https://edpb.europa.eu/system/files/2021-10/es_final_decision_bcr-c_colt_group_20210804_en.pdf">EDPB website.</a></p>
<p>The Binding Corporate Rules ("BCRs") are the golden privacy certification approved by three European Data Protection Authorities as well as the European Data Protection Board which allows:</p>
<ul>
<li>Colt to have the highest recognition in privacy that a group of companies can have</li>
<li>Transfer of personal data easily between all Colt´s entities</li>
<li>Keeping the same levels and standards of privacy compliance all over Colt worldwide</li>
</ul>
</div>
	</div>
</div>

<div class="fl-col-group fl-node-622f223dc7069 fl-col-group-nested" data-node="622f223dc7069">
			<div class="fl-col fl-node-622f223dc7816 fl-col-small" data-node="622f223dc7816">
	<div class="fl-col-content fl-node-content">		<div class="fl-module fl-module-button fl-node-61bb1dd80a8fe" data-node="61bb1dd80a8fe">
	<div class="fl-module-content fl-node-content">
		<div class="fl-button-wrap fl-button-width-auto fl-button-left">
			<a href="https://www.colt.net/wp-content/uploads/2022/05/Colt-BCRS-01.pdf" target="_blank" class="fl-button" role="button" rel="noopener">
							<span class="fl-button-text">Download our BCRs infographic</span>
					</a>
</div>
	</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
			<div class="fl-col fl-node-622f223dc781a" data-node="622f223dc781a">
	<div class="fl-col-content fl-node-content">		<div class="fl-module fl-module-button fl-node-622f224b8fe2b" data-node="622f224b8fe2b">
	<div class="fl-module-content fl-node-content">
		<div class="fl-button-wrap fl-button-width-auto fl-button-left">
			<a href="https://www.colt.net/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Colt-BCR-Controller-Approved.pdf" target="_blank" class="fl-button" role="button" rel="noopener">
							<span class="fl-button-text">Colt BCR Controller Approved</span>

<div class="fl-module fl-module-button fl-node-622f22405253b" data-node="622f22405253b">
	<div class="fl-module-content fl-node-content">
		<div class="fl-button-wrap fl-button-width-auto fl-button-left">
			<a href="https://www.colt.net/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Colt-BCR-Processor-Approved.pdf" target="_blank" class="fl-button" role="button" rel="noopener">
							<span class="fl-button-text">Colt BCR Processor Approved</span>
					</a>
</div>

<div class="fl-module fl-module-accordion fl-node-61bb1c39831bf" data-node="61bb1c39831bf">
	<div class="fl-module-content fl-node-content">
		
<div class="fl-accordion fl-accordion-small fl-accordion-collapse" role="tablist">
				<div class="fl-accordion-item ">
				<div class="fl-accordion-button" id="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-tab-0" aria-selected="false" aria-controls="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-panel-0" aria-expanded="false" role="tab" tabindex="0">

					
					<a href="#" id="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-label-0" class="fl-accordion-button-label" tabindex="0" aria-controls="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-panel-0">What are the Binding Corporate Rules?</a>

											<a href="#" id="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-icon-0" class="fl-accordion-button-icon" tabindex="0" aria-controls="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-panel-0"><i class="fl-accordion-button-icon fl-accordion-button-icon-right fas fa-plus"><span class="sr-only">Expand</span></i></a>
					
				</div>
				<div class="fl-accordion-content fl-clearfix" id="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-panel-0" aria-labelledby="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-tab-0" aria-hidden="true" role="tabpanel" aria-live="polite">
					<p>The Binding Corporate Rules (“BCRs”) are a certification granted by the European Data Protection Board (“EDPB”), the collective body of all EU Data Protection Authorities. Through the BCRs, the EDPB certifythat the privacy programme implemented by a company is compliant with the General Data Protection Regulations (“GDPR”)and the same level of data protection compliance valid in Europe is applied all over the entities of the same group. In addition, the BCRs are a tool for safely transfer personal data outside the EU within a group of companies.</p>
				</div>
			</div>
						<div class="fl-accordion-item ">
				<div class="fl-accordion-button" id="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-tab-1" aria-selected="false" aria-controls="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-panel-1" aria-expanded="false" role="tab" tabindex="0">

					
					<a href="#" id="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-label-1" class="fl-accordion-button-label" tabindex="0" aria-controls="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-panel-1">Are the BCRs a privacy compliance tool?</a>

											<a href="#" id="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-icon-1" class="fl-accordion-button-icon" tabindex="0" aria-controls="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-panel-1"><i class="fl-accordion-button-icon fl-accordion-button-icon-right fas fa-plus"><span class="sr-only">Expand</span></i></a>
					
				</div>
				<div class="fl-accordion-content fl-clearfix" id="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-panel-1" aria-labelledby="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-tab-1" aria-hidden="true" role="tabpanel" aria-live="polite">
					<p>Yes, the BCR are the only available instrument to get company ́s data privacy practices comprehensively approved by the EU Data Protection Authorities.</p>
				</div>
			</div>
						<div class="fl-accordion-item ">
				<div class="fl-accordion-button" id="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-tab-2" aria-selected="false" aria-controls="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-panel-2" aria-expanded="false" role="tab" tabindex="0">

					
					<a href="#" id="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-label-2" class="fl-accordion-button-label" tabindex="0" aria-controls="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-panel-2">When was Colt awarded the BCRs?</a>

											<a href="#" id="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-icon-2" class="fl-accordion-button-icon" tabindex="0" aria-controls="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-panel-2"><i class="fl-accordion-button-icon fl-accordion-button-icon-right fas fa-plus"><span class="sr-only">Expand</span></i></a>
					
				</div>
				<div class="fl-accordion-content fl-clearfix" id="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-panel-2" aria-labelledby="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-tab-2" aria-hidden="true" role="tabpanel" aria-live="polite">
					<p>Colt BCRs controller and processor have been approved by the European Data Protection Board (EDPB) August 2nd, 2021. The approval waspublished in the official Gazette of the EDPB on August 5th, 2021 and ratified by the Spanish Data Protection Authority, as Colt ́s BCR leading Authority August 16th, 2021.</p>
				</div>
			</div>
						<div class="fl-accordion-item ">
				<div class="fl-accordion-button" id="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-tab-3" aria-selected="false" aria-controls="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-panel-3" aria-expanded="false" role="tab" tabindex="0">

					
					<a href="#" id="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-label-3" class="fl-accordion-button-label" tabindex="0" aria-controls="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-panel-3">What does the BCRs imply for Colt?</a>

											<a href="#" id="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-icon-3" class="fl-accordion-button-icon" tabindex="0" aria-controls="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-panel-3"><i class="fl-accordion-button-icon fl-accordion-button-icon-right fas fa-plus"><span class="sr-only">Expand</span></i></a>
					
				</div>
				<div class="fl-accordion-content fl-clearfix" id="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-panel-3" aria-labelledby="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-tab-3" aria-hidden="true" role="tabpanel" aria-live="polite">
					<div class="page" data-page-number="1" data-loaded="true">
<div class="textLayer">Colt's BCRs allow Colt to transfer EU personal data within the Group, even outside the EEA, recognizing a Global Privacy programme that meets highest possible industry standards.</div>
</div>
<div class="page" data-page-number="2" data-loaded="true">
<div class="canvasWrapper"></div>
<div class="textLayer">For approving our BCRS, the EDPB audited, validated and approved Colt privacy compliance framework applicable in all Colt ́s entities. With them, Colt can offer the best data protection assurance in the world.</div>
</div>
				</div>
			</div>
						<div class="fl-accordion-item ">
				<div class="fl-accordion-button" id="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-tab-4" aria-selected="false" aria-controls="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-panel-4" aria-expanded="false" role="tab" tabindex="0">

					
					<a href="#" id="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-label-4" class="fl-accordion-button-label" tabindex="0" aria-controls="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-panel-4">Are the BCRs applicable over all Colt entities?</a>

											<a href="#" id="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-icon-4" class="fl-accordion-button-icon" tabindex="0" aria-controls="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-panel-4"><i class="fl-accordion-button-icon fl-accordion-button-icon-right fas fa-plus"><span class="sr-only">Expand</span></i></a>
					
				</div>
				<div class="fl-accordion-content fl-clearfix" id="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-panel-4" aria-labelledby="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-tab-4" aria-hidden="true" role="tabpanel" aria-live="polite">
					<p>The EDPB approved the Privacy and GDPR compliance programme implemented by Colt across the whole group. The approved privacy programme is legally binding on every company of the group.</p>
				</div>
			</div>
						<div class="fl-accordion-item ">
				<div class="fl-accordion-button" id="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-tab-5" aria-selected="false" aria-controls="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-panel-5" aria-expanded="false" role="tab" tabindex="0">

					
					<a href="#" id="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-label-5" class="fl-accordion-button-label" tabindex="0" aria-controls="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-panel-5">Are there any other Telco companies which have obtained the BCRS post-GDPR? </a>

											<a href="#" id="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-icon-5" class="fl-accordion-button-icon" tabindex="0" aria-controls="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-panel-5"><i class="fl-accordion-button-icon fl-accordion-button-icon-right fas fa-plus"><span class="sr-only">Expand</span></i></a>
					
				</div>
				<div class="fl-accordion-content fl-clearfix" id="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-panel-5" aria-labelledby="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-tab-5" aria-hidden="true" role="tabpanel" aria-live="polite">
					<p>At the moment, Colt is the only Telco in the market with the BCRs. This gives Colt a competitive advantage before our competitors. The BCRs are considered the top privacy compliance standard. With the BCRs, Colt can offer the best data protection assurance standard in the world.</p>
				</div>
			</div>
						<div class="fl-accordion-item ">
				<div class="fl-accordion-button" id="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-tab-6" aria-selected="false" aria-controls="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-panel-6" aria-expanded="false" role="tab" tabindex="0">

					
					<a href="#" id="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-label-6" class="fl-accordion-button-label" tabindex="0" aria-controls="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-panel-6">Please could you explain a little the procedure of obtaining the BCRs?</a>

											<a href="#" id="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-icon-6" class="fl-accordion-button-icon" tabindex="0" aria-controls="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-panel-6"><i class="fl-accordion-button-icon fl-accordion-button-icon-right fas fa-plus"><span class="sr-only">Expand</span></i></a>
					
				</div>
				<div class="fl-accordion-content fl-clearfix" id="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-panel-6" aria-labelledby="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-tab-6" aria-hidden="true" role="tabpanel" aria-live="polite">
					<p>Colt BCRs were negotiated and discussed with the 3 toughest European Data Protection Authorities and approved by the European Data Protection Boardwhich includes all the EU Data Protection Authorities. The Italian Data Protection Authority was the “guardian” of such procedure. This approval proves that Colt has implemented the most stringent privacy rules on the European scene and worldwide.</p>
				</div>
			</div>
						<div class="fl-accordion-item ">
				<div class="fl-accordion-button" id="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-tab-7" aria-selected="false" aria-controls="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-panel-7" aria-expanded="false" role="tab" tabindex="0">

					
					<a href="#" id="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-label-7" class="fl-accordion-button-label" tabindex="0" aria-controls="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-panel-7">Where can you find the official approval of Colt BCR?</a>

											<a href="#" id="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-icon-7" class="fl-accordion-button-icon" tabindex="0" aria-controls="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-panel-7"><i class="fl-accordion-button-icon fl-accordion-button-icon-right fas fa-plus"><span class="sr-only">Expand</span></i></a>
					
				</div>
				<div class="fl-accordion-content fl-clearfix" id="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-panel-7" aria-labelledby="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-tab-7" aria-hidden="true" role="tabpanel" aria-live="polite">
					<p>Colt BCR Controller and Processor decisions are published at the European Data Protection Board (EDPB) website:<br>
<a href="https://edpb.europa.eu/our-work-tools/accountability-tools/bcr_en">https://edpb.europa.eu/our-work-tools/accountability-tools/bcr_en</a></p>
<p>Spanish Data Protection Authority (“AEPD”) website:<br>
<a href="https://www.aepd.es/es/documento/ti-00003-2021-resolucion-aprobacion-bcr-responsable-colt.pdf">https://www.aepd.es/es/documento/ti-00003-2021-resolucion-aprobacion-bcr-responsable-colt.pdf</a></p>
				</div>
			</div>
						<div class="fl-accordion-item ">
				<div class="fl-accordion-button" id="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-tab-8" aria-selected="false" aria-controls="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-panel-8" aria-expanded="false" role="tab" tabindex="0">

					
					<a href="#" id="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-label-8" class="fl-accordion-button-label" tabindex="0" aria-controls="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-panel-8">Individual rights</a>

											<a href="#" id="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-icon-8" class="fl-accordion-button-icon" tabindex="0" aria-controls="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-panel-8"><i class="fl-accordion-button-icon fl-accordion-button-icon-right fas fa-plus"><span class="sr-only">Expand</span></i></a>
					
				</div>
				<div class="fl-accordion-content fl-clearfix" id="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-panel-8" aria-labelledby="fl-accordion-61bb1c39831bf-tab-8" aria-hidden="true" role="tabpanel" aria-live="polite">
					<p>Colt shall inform all individuals about how to exercise their rights and ensure that individuals are able to exercise their rights freely. Colt will respond as appropriate to requests to exercise any of the following individual rights:</p>
<p>(a) Right of access: Individuals have the right to access a copy of the personal data that has been collected about them (whether held by Colt itself or at its providers), and be provided with information about the processing.</p>
<p>(b) Right of rectification: Individuals have the right to rectify any inaccurate or incomplete personal data concerning them (whether held by Colt itself or at its providers), in order to guarantee their accuracy and the appropriate processing thereof.</p>
<p>(c) Right of erasure (right to be forgotten): Individuals have the right to the deletion of personal data concerning them.</p>
<p>(d) Right to object: Individuals have the right to object to the processing of personal data at any time.</p>
<p>(e) Right of restriction: Individuals have the right to restrict the processing of personal data concerning him or her. This means that the processing will be "paused" and the personal data will only be stored.</p>
<p>(f) Right of data portability: Individuals have the right to receive personal data concerning them and to have that data transmitted to another controller in a structured, commonly used, machine-readable format.</p>
<p>(g) Right to non-automated data processing: Individuals have the right not to be subject to a decision affecting them, where this decision is based on automated data processing of information, including profiles. This includes cases in which Colt uses cookies as a technical tool to evaluate customers and predict their behaviour, performance or preferences, comparing their profile with that of other users or similar customers.</p>
<p>7.10.2 Colt responds to these requests in accordance with the procedure provided by the Individual Rights Policy</p>
				</div>
			</div>

<div class="fl-module fl-module-heading fl-node-5f0d77d9af0f4" data-node="5f0d77d9af0f4">
	<div class="fl-module-content fl-node-content">
		<h3 class="fl-heading">
		<span class="fl-heading-text">Key points you need to know about how we collect and use your data</span>
	</h3>
	</div>
</div>
<div class="fl-module fl-module-rich-text fl-node-5f0d77d9af0f5" data-node="5f0d77d9af0f5">
	<div class="fl-module-content fl-node-content">
		<div class="fl-rich-text">
	<p>We collect and use your personal data to administer our relationship with you, including to respond to your enquiries or complaints, to provide our products and Services to you, to manage our Contracts with you, to inform you about our products and services, partners, promotions and events, to administer and improve our Websites and Services, to respond to requests from authorities, to comply with our contractual and legal obligations, and for other legitimate business purposes. Colt does not share, sell, rent or trade personal data with third parties for promotional purposes.</p>
<p>When you express an interest in obtaining additional information about the Services, or registering to use the Web sites or other Services, or registering for an event, you provide the Company with personal contact information, such as name, company name, address, phone number, and email address (“Required Contact Information”) to contact you. In addition, when you purchase the Services or get registered for an event, Colt may also require you to provide the Company with means for financial qualification and billing information, such as billing name and address, and the number of employees within the organization that will be using the Services (“Billing Information”) which is not considered personal data.</p>
<p>We may ask you for information to enable us to provide a Service to you and we collect this information by telephone, written/digital correspondence or via the website.</p>
<p>Subject to your consent where required by law, we use cookies and other technologies to track the use of our websites and services. To learn about our use of cookies and your rights in that respect see below.</p>
<p>Subject to your consent where required by law, we may use your personal data to conduct marketing, promotional and informational activities and to perform business analytics, satisfaction surveys or market research and conduct direct marketing.</p>
<p>We may share your personal data with other entities of the Colt group of companies, with third party providers that we engage to process data on our behalf, when such sharing is required by law or other situations as permitted by law. In accordance with applicable law, you have the right to access personal data we hold about you, to rectify, delete or erase inaccurate data, to object, at any time and free of charge, to the processing of your personal data for direct marketing purposes, as well other rights under applicable law.</p>
<p>Your use of our Services and Websites, and the entering into our Contracts, constitute your consent to the processing and transfer of your personal data to India and to other Colt's entities which are located in other jurisdictions outside of the European Economic Area which may not provide the same level of data protection as your home country.</p>
<p>This privacy policy only applies to how to Colt deals with your personal data. It does not apply to any to any other company or to any other company´s websites even if you have accessed them through Colt. If you disclose your personal data to other companies your information will be dealt with according to their privacy practices.</p>
</div>
	</div>
</div>
<div class="fl-module fl-module-accordion fl-node-5f0d77d9af0fb" data-node="5f0d77d9af0fb">
	<div class="fl-module-content fl-node-content">
		
<div class="fl-accordion fl-accordion-small fl-accordion-collapse" role="tablist">
				<div class="fl-accordion-item ">
				<div class="fl-accordion-button" id="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0fb-tab-0" aria-selected="false" aria-controls="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0fb-panel-0" aria-expanded="false" role="tab" tabindex="0">

					
					<a href="#" id="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0fb-label-0" class="fl-accordion-button-label" tabindex="0" aria-controls="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0fb-panel-0">What personal data will Colt collect?</a>

											<a href="#" id="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0fb-icon-0" class="fl-accordion-button-icon" tabindex="0" aria-controls="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0fb-panel-0"><i class="fl-accordion-button-icon fl-accordion-button-icon-right fas fa-plus"><span class="sr-only">Expand</span></i></a>
					
				</div>
				<div class="fl-accordion-content fl-clearfix" id="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0fb-panel-0" aria-labelledby="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0fb-tab-0" aria-hidden="true" role="tabpanel" aria-live="polite">
					<p>For the purposes of this Privacy Policy, "personal data" means any information that identifies you, that could be used to identify you or that relates to you, and that you submit about you when interacting with us and/or is otherwise collected by us when you visit the Websites, by phone through our customer service, by writing through order forms or in another manner. During our relationship with you we may collect and process your personal data, such as your name, address, telephone, email and other contact details, and any other information relating to you which you may provide, in the following cases:</p>
<ul>
<li>Visit our Websites and look at our Products and Services</li>
<li>Create an account on our Websites</li>
<li>Enquire about our products and Services or contact our customer service</li>
<li>Enter into a Contract with us and purchase our products and Services</li>
<li>Participate in a promotion, event, survey or other marketing campaign we organise</li>
<li>Sign up for our newsletters and other promotional materials.<strong>&nbsp;</strong></li>
</ul>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p><strong>Personal Data that you provide us </strong></p>
<p>The types of personal data we may obtain in connection with the previous cases are as follows:</p>
<ul>
<li>Your name, address, and contact details (such as telephone, mobile and fax numbers, email address)</li>
<li>Details of contact persons (such as name, address, function/title, telephone and fax numbers, e-mail address)</li>
<li>Services provided, including online Services</li>
<li>Names, email addresses and telephone numbers of third parties you provide to us</li>
<li>Online account details including username, password and other credentials used to access Colt’s products and Services</li>
<li>Financial and payment data such as banking details, invoices and payment terms as well as any personal data for fulfilling and legitimate processing billing information</li>
<li>Complaints and enquiries</li>
<li>Business profile</li>
<li>Tax identification number where you request products or services that require such information</li>
<li>Responses provided in response to surveys</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>&nbsp;</strong></p>
<p><strong>Personal Data collected by automated means</strong></p>
<p>When you visit our Websites or use our Services, subject to your prior consent where applicable by law, we may collect personal data without you actively submitting such information, by automated means, using technologies such as cookies, web server logs, web beacons, and similar technologies as described below.</p>
<p>The types of personal data that we may collect through your visits to the Websites or use of the Services include, to the extent permitted under applicable law and, where required, subject to your express consent, are:</p>
<ul>
<li>the date and time of visit, referring address (location from which a visitor comes to the Websites);</li>
<li>type of Internet browser, OS and device details;</li>
<li>visitor's IP address (a unique number that is assigned to any computer that connects to the Internet for identification purposes);</li>
<li>traffic data for calls or Internet session when you use our phone or Internet services, including called numbers, identification of the phone, duration of the call, date, duration and data volume of the Internet session;</li>
<li>as the case may arise location data generated during calls or Internet sessions;</li>
<li>history of the contact you have had with our customer service.</li>
</ul>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p><strong>Personal Data collected by third parties</strong></p>
<p>Colt may also receive information about Customers from other sources, including third parties from whom we have purchased data, and combine this information with Data we already have about you.&nbsp; This helps us to update, expand and analyse our records, identify new customers, and create more tailored advertising to provide products and services that may be of interest to you. We will ensure that any marketing campaigns are aligned to GDPR requirements.</p>
				</div>
			</div>
						<div class="fl-accordion-item ">
				<div class="fl-accordion-button" id="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0fb-tab-1" aria-selected="false" aria-controls="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0fb-panel-1" aria-expanded="false" role="tab" tabindex="0">

					
					<a href="#" id="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0fb-label-1" class="fl-accordion-button-label" tabindex="0" aria-controls="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0fb-panel-1">How do we use your personal data?</a>

											<a href="#" id="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0fb-icon-1" class="fl-accordion-button-icon" tabindex="0" aria-controls="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0fb-panel-1"><i class="fl-accordion-button-icon fl-accordion-button-icon-right fas fa-plus"><span class="sr-only">Expand</span></i></a>
					
				</div>
				<div class="fl-accordion-content fl-clearfix" id="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0fb-panel-1" aria-labelledby="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0fb-tab-1" aria-hidden="true" role="tabpanel" aria-live="polite">
					<p>Colt shall only process your personal data for the purposes described in this Privacy Policy or as otherwise permitted under applicable law. The processing of your personal data by Colt for the purposes described hereunder is based on your explicit consent or on the necessity to process your personal data for the purposes of our legitimate interests, as provided by Article 9, 2., (a) and (f) of the General Data Protection Regulation (EU) 2016/679 of 27 April 2016 (“GDPR”).</p>
<p>Your personal information may be processed, both by Colt and its affiliates, for purposes including:</p>
<ul>
<li>administer our relationship with you, including to respond to your inquiries or complaints;</li>
<li>to provide any goods, Services or information you have requested and information about our products and Services;</li>
<li>to administer, operate, maintain, and improve the Websites and our Services;</li>
<li>for efficient customer management relationship;</li>
<li>to simplify access to some interactive features on our Websites or Services;</li>
<li>to manage your accounts, orders, invoices and payments;</li>
<li>to manage and provide after-sale services;</li>
<li>to administer accounting and taxes;</li>
<li>to respond to requests from administrative or judicial authorities; and</li>
<li>to comply with applicable laws and regulations.</li>
</ul>
<p>Providing personal data for these purposes is necessary and refusal would make it impossible for Colt to manage the Contract with you or to comply with its contractual and legal obligations. Subject to your consent where required by law, we may also use your personal data in order:</p>
<ul>
<li>to keep improving the way our website works.</li>
<li>to count how many persons visit our websites, where they come from, when they visit, how long they stay and what pages they look at.</li>
<li>to associate your activity on our website in order to give us insights into products and services you might like and measure how our advertising performs</li>
<li>to note browser, OS and device details used to make sure you get a good online experience when you access our websites.</li>
<li>to provide you access to valuable Colt internet-based information and Services;</li>
<li>to audit usage of the Websites;</li>
<li>to market and improve the Services that we offer; and</li>
<li>to conduct promotions campaigns, survey and other marketing initiatives pursuant to the "How do we use your personal data for marketing purposes?" section to follow.</li>
<li>Let you know about other offers and discounts</li>
<li>Understand how you use products &amp; services to develop newer &amp; better versions</li>
<li>Carry out research and statistical analysis including to monitor how all customers use our network, products and services on an anonymous or business by business basis</li>
<li>Prevent and detect fraud or other crimes, recover debts or trace those who owe us money</li>
</ul>
<p>Providing personal data for marketing purposes is optional and refusal will have no consequence on the performance of any Contract by Colt.</p>
<p>In order to provide you with a better experience and to improve the quality of our Services, to the fullest extent permitted by applicable law, we may combine the information you submit to us with other information that we may receive from you, from third parties, or with other public demographic information.</p>
<p>In addition, we collect information from visitors to our websites to help us to make improvements to the websites and to the Services we make available. We know, for instance, how many visitors there are to each website page, when they visited, for how long and to which areas of the website. We may share this information with our advertisers and to other companies that offer their goods or services on our websites. It helps us to show these organisations how effective our website is as a sales channel for products. You or any other individual cannot be identified from the information we share as the data is aggregated and anonymised.</p>
				</div>
			</div>
						<div class="fl-accordion-item ">
				<div class="fl-accordion-button" id="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0fb-tab-2" aria-selected="false" aria-controls="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0fb-panel-2" aria-expanded="false" role="tab" tabindex="0">

					
					<a href="#" id="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0fb-label-2" class="fl-accordion-button-label" tabindex="0" aria-controls="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0fb-panel-2">Why and with whom do we share your personal data?</a>

											<a href="#" id="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0fb-icon-2" class="fl-accordion-button-icon" tabindex="0" aria-controls="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0fb-panel-2"><i class="fl-accordion-button-icon fl-accordion-button-icon-right fas fa-plus"><span class="sr-only">Expand</span></i></a>
					
				</div>
				<div class="fl-accordion-content fl-clearfix" id="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0fb-panel-2" aria-labelledby="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0fb-tab-2" aria-hidden="true" role="tabpanel" aria-live="polite">
					<p>Our policy is to not give, sell or otherwise distribute personal data we collect to third parties outside of Colt, except where required with your express consent or where this is necessary and in accordance with applicable law. In line with this, we share personal data with the recipients listed below.</p>
<p>Colt subsidiaries and affiliated entities (‘Colt Affiliates’). We may share your personal data with other companies of the Colt Group (a list of Colt Affiliates is available at https://www.colt.net/legal/ and then selecting the option Colt Group of Companies.&nbsp; For the purposes specified under the "How do we use this information?" section previous and as described under the "Will Personal Data be transferred abroad?" section in this document.</p>
<p>Third party service providers. Your personal data may be disclosed to third party service providers, acting on our behalf, in connection with managing services, data analytics, finance, accounting or other administrative services and information technology support. These third party service providers will have access to – and process – personal data only on our behalf and under our instructions and will be held to appropriate security obligations.</p>
<p>Colt’s business partners. A list of such partners could be provided to Customers upon request provided there is a legitimate reason.</p>
<p>Other data recipients. For the above purposes or where otherwise required by law, we may also need to make personal data available to third parties such as advisors, banks and financial institutions, professionals, independent consultants, potential or existing investors and/or acquirers (in connection with a merger, acquisition, or sale involving Colt or its affiliates or as part of a corporate reorganization, stock or asset sale, or other change in corporate control), regulatory and/or administrative authorities, courts, police authorities</p>
<p>Colt may provide information, in response to properly made requests, for the purposes of the prevention and detection of crime, and the apprehension or prosecution of offenders, when required to do so by law, for example under a court order, or in response to properly made court or administrative demands. Colt may also provide information for the purpose of safeguarding national security. In either case, Colt will act in accordance with applicable Data Protection Law.</p>
<p>Other telecommunications operators. Colt receives information from other telecommunications operators about their customers to enable Colt to enter their details (together with our own customer´s information) in telephone directories. We also make telephone numbers available on directory enquiry services unless customers (BT or other licensed telecommunications operators) have chosen to be ex-directory.</p>
<p>We may also disclose personal data about you when you explicitly consent (via contract or other legal instrument) to such transfer or when we believe disclosure is necessary or appropriate for our legitimate interests (or those of the third party to whom we disclose your data), provided that they are not overridden by the data subject's interests or fundamental rights and freedoms, in accordance with applicable laws.</p>
<p>We may share with third parties certain pieces of aggregated, non-personal information, such as how our customers use of our Services or Websites. Such information would not identify you individually.</p>
<p>Please note that when you order goods and services from Colt, the Company may make enquiries about you for credit reference purposes. These enquires include searching your records held by a credit reference agency. At all times where your information is disclosed to us we will protect it in accordance with this policy and keep it secure.</p>
				</div>
			</div>
						<div class="fl-accordion-item ">
				<div class="fl-accordion-button" id="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0fb-tab-3" aria-selected="false" aria-controls="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0fb-panel-3" aria-expanded="false" role="tab" tabindex="0">

					
					<a href="#" id="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0fb-label-3" class="fl-accordion-button-label" tabindex="0" aria-controls="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0fb-panel-3">Will personal data be transferred abroad?</a>

											<a href="#" id="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0fb-icon-3" class="fl-accordion-button-icon" tabindex="0" aria-controls="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0fb-panel-3"><i class="fl-accordion-button-icon fl-accordion-button-icon-right fas fa-plus"><span class="sr-only">Expand</span></i></a>
					
				</div>
				<div class="fl-accordion-content fl-clearfix" id="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0fb-panel-3" aria-labelledby="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0fb-tab-3" aria-hidden="true" role="tabpanel" aria-live="polite">
					<p>In the performance of our Contract with you or in providing our Services or Websites to you, we may need to transfer your personal data to Colt Affiliates, business Partners or other recipients identified in the "Why and with whom do we share your personal data?" section previous that are located inside and outside the European Economic Area (“EEA”), including in countries that do not provide the same level of protection for personal data as in the EEA. In any case, we will only transfer personal data to recipients that provide an adequate level of data protection or as permitted by applicable data protection laws by implementing appropriate safeguards, including, but not limited to, relevant data transfer agreements. Colt has implemented an IGTA (International Group Transfer Agreement) based on Model Clauses contract, which makes Colt compliant with GDPR International Transfer Data Protection Rules, Brexit and Privacy Shield null declaration. The<strong> IGTA</strong> standardizes the governance around the transfer of personal data between Colt entities and includes standard contractual clauses approved by the European Commission (“Model Clauses”).</p>
<p>Colt BCRs controller and processor have been approved by the European Data Protection Board (EDPB) August 02, 2021. The approval was published in the official Gazette of the EDPB on August 05, 2021 and ratified by the Spanish Data Protection Authority, as Colt ́s BCR leading Authority August 16, 2021. The EDPB approved the Privacy and GDPR compliance programme implemented by Colt across the whole group. The approved privacy programme is legally binding on every company of the group.</p>
<p>Colt BCR Controller and Processor decisions are published at the European Data Protection Board(EDPB) website <a href="https://edpb.europa.eu/our-work-tools/accountability-tools/bcr_en">https://edpb.europa.eu/our-work-tools/accountability-tools/bcr_en</a> and in the Spanish Data Protection Authority (“AEPD”) website: <a href="https://www.aepd.es/es/documento/ti-00003-2021-resolucion-aprobacion-bcr-responsable-colt.pdf">https://www.aepd.es/es/documento/ti-00003-2021-resolucion-aprobacion-bcr-responsable-colt.pdf</a></p>
<p>The Binding Corporate Rules ("BCRs") are the golden privacy certification approved by three European Data Protection Authorities as well as the European Data Protection Board which allows:</p>
<p>• Colt to have the highest recognition in privacy that a group of companies can have.<br>
• Transfer of personal data easily between all Colt´s entities.<br>
• Keeping the same levels and standards of privacy compliance all over Colt worldwide.</p>
<div>Please be aware that the personal data (e.g. your name and email address) you may provide through the chat bot available at the portal <u><a tabindex="-1" title="https://online.colt.net/" href="https://online.colt.net/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">https://online.colt.net/</a></u> will be stored at Google LLC Cloud servers in US. You are informed before you interact with the chat bot and should you not wish to continue, you can close the chat bot. Adequate international data transfer safeguards and security measures have been implemented to keep your personal data safe and secure. For further information on how Google secures your data please visit <u><a tabindex="-1" title="https://cloud.google.com/security/gdpr/resource-center" href="https://cloud.google.com/security/gdpr/resource-center" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">https://cloud.google.com/security/gdpr/resource-center</a></u>.</div>
				</div>
			</div>
						<div class="fl-accordion-item ">
				<div class="fl-accordion-button" id="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0fb-tab-4" aria-selected="false" aria-controls="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0fb-panel-4" aria-expanded="false" role="tab" tabindex="0">

					
					<a href="#" id="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0fb-label-4" class="fl-accordion-button-label" tabindex="0" aria-controls="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0fb-panel-4">Colt Vendor Risk Management Procedure</a>

											<a href="#" id="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0fb-icon-4" class="fl-accordion-button-icon" tabindex="0" aria-controls="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0fb-panel-4"><i class="fl-accordion-button-icon fl-accordion-button-icon-right fas fa-plus"><span class="sr-only">Expand</span></i></a>
					
				</div>
				<div class="fl-accordion-content fl-clearfix" id="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0fb-panel-4" aria-labelledby="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0fb-tab-4" aria-hidden="true" role="tabpanel" aria-live="polite">
					<p>As part of Colt´s Privacy Governance Policy, Colt ensures vendors privacy compliance through a Vendor Risk Assessment Tool to implement a Vendor Data Privacy Due Diligence including appropriate security, technical and organisational measures and legal checking. Once the Privacy Due Diligence is positively completed, prior to sharing any personal data with vendors, a Data Processing Agreement containing all the requirement stipulated in Article 28 of the GDPR is executed between the parties. In addition, if any personal data needs to be transferred to a third country outside the European Union, as per Article 46 of the GDPR, Model Clauses are executed between the parties involved to assure that personal data is processed with the same level of protection that in the European Union. Furthermore, Colt reviews vendor status on Data Protection at contract renewal and carries out audits to check vendors privacy compliance.</p>
				</div>
			</div>
						<div class="fl-accordion-item ">

											<a href="#" id="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0fb-icon-5" class="fl-accordion-button-icon" tabindex="0" aria-controls="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0fb-panel-5"><i class="fl-accordion-button-icon fl-accordion-button-icon-right fas fa-plus"><span class="sr-only">Expand</span></i></a>
					
				</div>
				<div class="fl-accordion-content fl-clearfix" id="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0fb-panel-5" aria-labelledby="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0fb-tab-5" aria-hidden="true" role="tabpanel" aria-live="polite">
					<p>Colt has appropriate policies and technical and organizational measures in place to safeguard and protect your personal data against unlawful or unauthorised access, accidental loss or destruction, damage, unlawful or unauthorised use and disclosure. We will also take all reasonable precautions to ensure that our staff and employees who have access to personal data about you have received adequate training.</p>

					<p>We have a retention policy for personal data that we adhere to, in line with legal and statutory requirements. For further details regarding this please contact the DPO (Data Protection Office) at Colt using the email address <a href="mailto:gdpr@colt.net">gdpr@colt.net</a>. We also may retain your information for the period of time needed for Colt to pursue legitimate business interests, conduct audits, comply with our legal obligations, resolve disputes and enforce our agreements.</p>

					<p>If you provide us with personal data about third parties, you warrant, represent, and undertake that you have complied with applicable data protection laws including informing and obtaining all necessary consents and approvals for the provision of such personal data to Colt and the processing by Colt of this personal data as described in this Privacy Policy.</p>

<p>When you register online for a Colt account, you can also view and update your personal data by logging onto the Website and following the relevant instructions. To ensure any details we hold about you remain accurate, please update your personal data if it changes or send a request to us as described under the "What are your data protection rights?" section below. If you close your account we may, for limited periods and in accordance with applicable law, retain some personal data in order to comply with legal obligations or for other proper purposes, such as legal retention obligations, collecting outstanding debts or resolving legal disputes.</p>
<p>When you request to be removed from certain marketing offers, you will, in accordance with applicable data protection laws, be added to the relevant internal suppression list(s) to ensure your request is complied with</p>

					<a href="#" id="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0fb-label-12" class="fl-accordion-button-label" tabindex="0" aria-controls="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0fb-panel-12">What are your data protection rights?</a>

											<a href="#" id="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0fb-icon-12" class="fl-accordion-button-icon" tabindex="0" aria-controls="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0fb-panel-12"><i class="fl-accordion-button-icon fl-accordion-button-icon-right fas fa-plus"><span class="sr-only">Expand</span></i></a>

				<div class="fl-accordion-content fl-clearfix" id="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0fb-panel-12" aria-labelledby="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0fb-tab-12" aria-hidden="true" role="tabpanel" aria-live="polite">
					<p>In accordance with applicable data protection law, you have a right to:</p>
<ul>
<li>obtain confirmation of the existence of, and to request a written copy of the personal information Colt holds about you.</li>
<li>have any inaccurate information about you corrected;</li>
<li>have personal data we hold about you deleted, blocked or removed;</li>
<li>withdraw your consent where relevant, without affecting the lawfulness of processing based on your consent before its withdrawal;</li>
<li>restrict the processing we make in relation with your personal data;</li>
<li>receive your personal data, which you have provided to us, in a structured, commonly used and machine-readable format in order to transmit them to another data controller;</li>
<li>object to the use of your details for marketing activities and other promotional activities, as described under the "How do we use your personal data for marketing purposes?" section previous; and</li>
<li>lodge a complaint with a supervisory authority, in particular in the Member State of your habitual residence, place of work or place of the alleged infringement if you consider that the processing of your personal data relating infringes applicable data protection law.</li>
</ul>
<p>In case you wish to exercise any such rights, please send a written and signed request to Colt as described under the "How can you contact us?" section below.</p>

Where appropriate or required by law, we will notify you about the new privacy Policy by posting appropriate notice on our Services or Website or by e-mail (to the extent that we have your e-mail address). <div id="cookies" class="fl-module fl-module-heading fl-node-5f0d77d9af0f9" data-node="5f0d77d9af0f9">
	<div class="fl-module-content fl-node-content">
		<h2 class="fl-heading">
		<span class="fl-heading-text">Cookies Policy</span>
	</h2>
	</div>
</div>
<div class="fl-module fl-module-rich-text fl-node-5f0d77d9af0fa" data-node="5f0d77d9af0fa">
	<div class="fl-module-content fl-node-content">
		<div class="fl-rich-text">
	<p>This Cookie Policy applies to all websites offered by Colt Technology Services Group Limited and, where applicable, any of its EU-based affiliates (hereinafter "Colt", "we" or "us"), which refer to this Cookie Policy. As this Cookie Policy applies to all of our websites (unless otherwise expressly provided), they are collectively referred to as “Websites” throughout this Cookie Policy.</p>
<p>When you visit our Websites we may use cookies or similar technologies as described below. By clicking on "continue" or "I accept" on the cookie banner which is presented to you,&nbsp;you are agreeing to our use of cookies in accordance with this Cookie Policy and you acknowledge that we will use the underlying personal data processing as we have set out here</p>
<p>If you do not agree to our use of cookies in this way, you should click "decline". You are also able to change your cookie choices by clicking on the relevant button. Please note, however, that disabling cookies might affect your online experience and/or prevent you from taking full advantage of our Websites.</p>
</div>
	</div>
</div>
<div class="fl-module fl-module-accordion fl-node-5f0d77d9af0f3" data-node="5f0d77d9af0f3">
	<div class="fl-module-content fl-node-content">
		
<div class="fl-accordion fl-accordion-small fl-accordion-collapse" role="tablist">
				<div class="fl-accordion-item ">
				<div class="fl-accordion-button" id="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0f3-tab-0" aria-selected="false" aria-controls="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0f3-panel-0" aria-expanded="false" role="tab" tabindex="0">

					
					<a href="#" id="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0f3-label-0" class="fl-accordion-button-label" tabindex="0" aria-controls="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0f3-panel-0">What are cookies?</a>

											<a href="#" id="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0f3-icon-0" class="fl-accordion-button-icon" tabindex="0" aria-controls="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0f3-panel-0"><i class="fl-accordion-button-icon fl-accordion-button-icon-right fas fa-plus"><span class="sr-only">Expand</span></i></a>
					
				</div>
				<div class="fl-accordion-content fl-clearfix" id="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0f3-panel-0" aria-labelledby="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0f3-tab-0" aria-hidden="true" role="tabpanel" aria-live="polite">
					<p>Cookies are files or pieces of information that may be stored on your hard drive or browser (or other internet enabled devices, such as a smartphone or tablet) when you visit the Website. A cookie will usually contain the name of the website from which the cookie has come from, the "lifetime" of the cookie (i.e. how long the cookie will remain on your device), and a value, which is usually a randomly generated unique number.</p>
<p>They enable our Websites to identify your computer, as you navigate different pages on a website, and recognise that you have visited before. Cookies themselves do not contain any directly identifiable personal information. However, we may link the information we store in cookies to any personally identifiable information you submit while on our Websites.</p>
<p>From time to time we may also use other technologies to log and collect data in order to analyse traffic to our Websites. These technologies will regularly only allow for a non-directly identifiable notice of your visit to be generated. However, in some instances they may allow us to obtain details about your IP address and to track visits to our Websites. In conjunction with cookies, this will enable us to identify what portions of our Websites are of interest to our visitors and to help us provide you with tailored information from our Websites.</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
				</div>
			</div>
						<div class="fl-accordion-item ">
				<div class="fl-accordion-button" id="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0f3-tab-1" aria-selected="false" aria-controls="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0f3-panel-1" aria-expanded="false" role="tab" tabindex="0">

					
					<a href="#" id="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0f3-label-1" class="fl-accordion-button-label" tabindex="0" aria-controls="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0f3-panel-1">For what purposes do our website use cookies?</a>

											<a href="#" id="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0f3-icon-1" class="fl-accordion-button-icon" tabindex="0" aria-controls="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0f3-panel-1"><i class="fl-accordion-button-icon fl-accordion-button-icon-right fas fa-plus"><span class="sr-only">Expand</span></i></a>
					
				</div>
				<div class="fl-accordion-content fl-clearfix" id="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0f3-panel-1" aria-labelledby="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0f3-tab-1" aria-hidden="true" role="tabpanel" aria-live="polite">
					<p>Many cookies on our Websites perform essential functions or services you have requested or for security purposes, as further described in the table below.</p>
<p>Cookies also help us understand which sections of our Websites are the most popular, as they help show which pages are being visited and how long for. This helps us adapt our Websites to provide more relevant and accessible information and to better tailor our Websites and our products and services to your interests and needs. For example, cookies allow us to ensure that the information displayed on your next visit to our Websites will match up with your user preferences.</p>
<p>Cookies may also be used to help speed up your future activities and experience on our Websites.</p>
<p>We also use cookies to show adverts that are more relevant to your interests for example, with your consent, we use tracking technologies to remember content that has interested you and then use this to help us serve more relevant ads to you, including when you are on another site. Tracking technologies also help limit the number of times that you see an ad, measure the effectiveness of advertising campaigns and help us and others track whether ads have been properly displayed so we can pay for this.</p>
<p>We also use cookies to compile non-directly identifiable, aggregated statistics that allow us to understand how users use our Websites and to help us improve the structure and content of the Websites (for example, by monitoring which features of the Websites are being used, which pages are visited, how often, and what information is downloaded).</p>
<p>In sum, advantages of cookies are:</p>
<ol>
<li>Remembering the details as provided by the user.</li>
<li>Remembering user preferences.</li>
<li>Helping improve the website.</li>
<li>Cookies can be deleted by the visitor.</li>
<li>Cookies cannot carry any threat to the visitor’s device.</li>
</ol>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
				</div>
			</div>
						<div class="fl-accordion-item ">
				<div class="fl-accordion-button" id="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0f3-tab-2" aria-selected="false" aria-controls="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0f3-panel-2" aria-expanded="false" role="tab" tabindex="0">

					
					<a href="#" id="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0f3-label-2" class="fl-accordion-button-label" tabindex="0" aria-controls="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0f3-panel-2">What type of Cookies Colt may place on your device</a>

											<a href="#" id="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0f3-icon-2" class="fl-accordion-button-icon" tabindex="0" aria-controls="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0f3-panel-2"><i class="fl-accordion-button-icon fl-accordion-button-icon-right fas fa-plus"><span class="sr-only">Expand</span></i></a>
					
				</div>
				<div class="fl-accordion-content fl-clearfix" id="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0f3-panel-2" aria-labelledby="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0f3-tab-2" aria-hidden="true" role="tabpanel" aria-live="polite">
					<ul>
<li><strong>Strictly necessary cookies</strong>: These cookies are essential in order for the operation of a website, such as cookies authenticating access to secure areas of the website. Without these cookies, services you have asked for cannot be provided.</li>
<li><strong>Session Cookies (Non-Persistent Cookies)</strong>: Session Cookies are the cookies which exist only while the user is on a particular website. These cookies are deleted once the user exits the web page, at the end of the browsing session.</li>
<li><strong>Persistent Cookies</strong>:&nbsp; Persistent Cookies are the cookies which remain on your device for a longer period of time, for the duration of each specific cookie, and will remain valid until its set expiry date (unless deleted by the user before the expiry date). They are used to recognize a return visitor as a unique user. If the visitor restricts persistent cookies, these cookies fail to gather any information about that visitor.</li>
<li><strong>Third Party Cookies</strong>: Certain third party cookies placed on your device are used for analytical and advertising purposes. These cookies can be persistent or non-persistent and are placed from different domain names. If you would like more information about these cookies, as well as information about how to consent or withdraw your consent for receiving such cookies, please see the table below and the links to these third parties’ privacy policies.</li>
</ul>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>When you visit the Websites, you may receive cookies from third party websites or domains. You should check the relevant third party's website for more information about these cookies. The relevant third party is responsible for providing you with information regarding the cookies they place and obtaining your consent before placing cookies on your device.</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>Personalization Cookies</strong>: These cookies enable our website to remember choices you made on the site, e.g. keeping a user logged in.</li>
<li><strong>Analytics Cookies</strong>: Analytics Cookies provide an aggregated view into site usage.</li>
<li><strong>Targeting or advertising cookies</strong>: These Cookies provide targeted advertising on the site or other sites.</li>
<li><strong>Social Media Cookies</strong>: These Cookies collect information when using social networking features on the site such as share or like.</li>
</ul>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
				</div>
			</div>
						<div class="fl-accordion-item ">
				<div class="fl-accordion-button" id="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0f3-tab-3" aria-selected="false" aria-controls="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0f3-panel-3" aria-expanded="false" role="tab" tabindex="0">

					
					<a href="#" id="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0f3-label-3" class="fl-accordion-button-label" tabindex="0" aria-controls="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0f3-panel-3">How can you control, delete or withdraw your consent to the use of cookies?</a>

											<a href="#" id="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0f3-icon-3" class="fl-accordion-button-icon" tabindex="0" aria-controls="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0f3-panel-3"><i class="fl-accordion-button-icon fl-accordion-button-icon-right fas fa-plus"><span class="sr-only">Expand</span></i></a>
					
				</div>
				<div class="fl-accordion-content fl-clearfix" id="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0f3-panel-3" aria-labelledby="fl-accordion-5f0d77d9af0f3-tab-3" aria-hidden="true" role="tabpanel" aria-live="polite">
					<p>You may withdraw your consent to our use of cookies on the Websites or delete or restrict the placing of cookies on your device by using our Cookie consent management platform by clicking the button below.</p>
<p><!-- OneTrust Cookies Settings button start --><button id="ot-sdk-btn" class="ot-sdk-show-settings">Configure</button><br>
<!-- OneTrust Cookies Settings button end --></p>
<p>If you disable the cookies that the Websites use, this may impact your experience while on the Websites, for example you may not be able to visit certain areas of the Websites or you may not receive personalised information when you visit the Websites.</p>
<p>You can also delete cookies already stored on your computer.</p>
<p>Again, doing this may have a negative impact on the usability of many websites.</p>
<p><strong><em>More Information</em></strong></p>
<p>For more information on cookies and their use visit:</p>
<p><u><a href="http://www.allaboutcookies.org/">http://www.allaboutcookies.org</a></u></p>
<p><u><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTTP_cookie">http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTTP_cookie</a></u></p>
<p>For more information on Data Protection, please refer to Colt's "<u><a href="https://www.colt.net/data-privacy-statement/">Privacy Statement</a></u>".</p>

	<div class="fl-module-content fl-node-content">
		<div class="fl-rich-text">
	<p>HubSpot</p>
</div>
	</div>
</div>
<div class="fl-module fl-module-rich-text fl-node-61bb2ace87a92" data-node="61bb2ace87a92">
	<div class="fl-module-content fl-node-content">
		<div class="fl-rich-text">
	<p>Cookie Purpose</p>
</div>
	</div>
</div>
<div class="fl-module fl-module-rich-text fl-node-61bb2ad0f3a4f" data-node="61bb2ad0f3a4f">
	<div class="fl-module-content fl-node-content">
		<div class="fl-rich-text">
	<p>Cookies collected by HubSpot are collected when browsing colt.net. When information is collected via a form submission, these details are built into an individual profile. HubSpot cookies are then used to know who has visited specific pages and downloaded specific content. Based off of your interactions on the site, and after you have entered your information into our site, some behaviour related information may be used to send you related email based content. You have the ability to be unsubscribed from these at any point should you wish to be. No personally identifyable information is collected about you by HubSpot, barring the information you give to us through our forms. Your cookie information will additionally be stored so that you do not have to fill out the same information again through forms.</p>
</div>
	</div>
</div>

																							</td>
																<td class="table-body-td   table-body-35" colspan="" rowspan=""><div class="table-header-th">
																			<span class="head-inner-text"> 
											
										<span> Expiry </span>

										
																	</span></div> 
																							<span class="content-text"> 1 day </span>
																							</td>
																<td class="table-body-td   table-body-36" colspan="" rowspan=""><div class="table-header-th">

										<span> What is this used for? </span>

										
																	</span></div>

																							</td>
											</tr></tbody>
				</table>
			</div>
		</div>
	</div>

<div id="actions" class="fl-module fl-module-heading fl-node-5f0d77d9af0fe" data-node="5f0d77d9af0fe">
	<div class="fl-module-content fl-node-content">
		<h2 class="fl-heading">
		<span class="fl-heading-text">Individual Rights</span>
	</h2>
	</div>
</div>
<div class="fl-module fl-module-heading fl-node-61bb1b2958af3" data-node="61bb1b2958af3">
	<div class="fl-module-content fl-node-content">
		<h2 class="fl-heading">
		<span class="fl-heading-text">For employees, former employees + candidates</span>
	</h2>
	</div>
</div>
<div class="fl-module fl-module-rich-text fl-node-61bb1b52af92f" data-node="61bb1b52af92f">
	<div class="fl-module-content fl-node-content">
		<div class="fl-rich-text">
	<p class="p1"><b>A) Data Subject Rights<br>
</b>Should you wish to exercise your privacy rights, please select and download the relevant form below and once completed, send it to <a href="mailto:HRContactCentre@Colt.net">HRContactCentre@Colt.net</a> together with a document that can identify you.</p>
<ul class="ul1">
<li><a href="https://www.colt.net/wp-content/uploads/2018/12/Request-form-Right-to-access.docx">Right to access</a></li>
<li><a href="https://www.colt.net/wp-content/uploads/2018/12/Request-form-Right-to-rectification.docx">Right to rectification</a></li>
<li><a href="https://www.colt.net/wp-content/uploads/2018/12/Request-form-Right-to-erasure.docx">Right to erasure</a></li>
<li><a href="https://www.colt.net/wp-content/uploads/2018/12/Request-form-Right-to-portability.docx">Right to portability</a></li>
<li class="li4"><a href="https://www.colt.net/wp-content/uploads/2018/12/Request-form-Right-to-restrict.docx"><span class="s3">Right to restrict</span></a></li>
<li class="li4"><a href="https://www.colt.net/wp-content/uploads/2018/12/Request-form-Right-to-object.docx"><span class="s3">Right to object</span></a></li>
<li class="li4"><a href="https://www.colt.net/wp-content/uploads/2018/12/Request-form-Right-to-Automated.docx"><span class="s3">Right to automated processing</span></a></li>
</ul>
<p class="p5">You can find more information about your Data Subject Rights <a href="https://www.colt.net/wp-content/uploads/2018/12/DSAR-FAQs.pdf"><span class="s4">here</span></a>.</p>
<p class="p5"><b>B) Data processing complaints<br>
</b>Should you wish to raise a complaint about your personal data, please download the form below and once completed, send it to <a href="mailto:HRContactCentre@Colt.net">HRContactCentre@Colt.net</a>&nbsp;together with a document that can identify you.</p>
<ul class="ul1">
<li class="li1"><a href="https://www.colt.net/wp-content/uploads/2018/12/Personal-Data-Complaint-Form.docx"><span class="s2">Complaint form</span></a></li>
</ul>
</div>
	</div>
</div>
<div class="fl-module fl-module-heading fl-node-61bb1b6cb5e29" data-node="61bb1b6cb5e29">
	<div class="fl-module-content fl-node-content">
		<h2 class="fl-heading">
		<span class="fl-heading-text">For customers</span>
	</h2>
	</div>

<div class="fl-module fl-module-rich-text fl-node-5f0d77d9af0e4" data-node="5f0d77d9af0e4">
	<div class="fl-module-content fl-node-content">
		<div class="fl-rich-text">
	<h4></h4>
<p><b>A) Data Subject Rights<br>
</b>Should you wish to exercise your privacy rights, please select and download the relevant form below and once completed, send it to <a href="mailto:GDPR@Colt.net">GDPR@Colt.net</a> together with a document that can identify you.</p>
<p>Should you wish to exercise your privacy rights relating to ticketing and invoicing, please select the relevant form below and raise a ticket in <a href="https://online.colt.net/">Colt Online</a>. You can track updates using your ticket reference in Colt Online.</p>
<ul>
<li><a href="https://dcp.colt.net/ticketingweb/raiseTicket?eid=Raccess" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Right to access</a></li>

<li class="li4"><a href="https://www.colt.net/wp-content/uploads/2018/12/Request-form-Right-to-object.docx"><span class="s3">Right to object</span></a></li>
<li class="li4"><a href="https://www.colt.net/wp-content/uploads/2018/12/Request-form-Right-to-Automated.docx"><span class="s3">Right to automated processing</span></a></li>
</ul>
<p class="p5"><b>B) Data processing complaints<br>
</b>Should you wish to raise a complaint about your personal data, please download the form below and once completed, send it to <a href="mailto:GDPR@Colt.net">GDPR@Colt.net</a> together with a document that can identify you.</p>
<ul class="ul1">

<p>If you have any data privacy questions or queries on other topics, please contact <a href="mailto:gdpr@colt.net" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-auth="NotApplicable">gdpr@colt.net.</a></p>
